import pandas as pd
import requests
from bs4 import BeautifulSoup
import sqlite3
# URL of the website
url = 'https://web.archive.org/web/20230902185655/https://en.everybodywiki.com/100_Most_Highly-Ranked_Films'
db_name = 'Movies.db'
table_name = 'Top_50'
csv_path = 'top_50_films.csv'
df = pd.DataFrame(columns=["Average Rank","Film","Year"])
count = 0 # Counter for the number of movies
html_page = requests.get(url).text
print(html_page)

                                <!-- title of the page -->
                                <h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading">100 Most Highly-Ranked Films</h1>
                                <!-- tagline; usually goes something like "From WikiName" primary purpose of this seems to be for printing to identify the source of the content -->
                                <div id="siteSub" class="siteSub">From EverybodyWiki Bios &amp; Wiki</div><div id="jump-to-nav" class="mw-jump jump-to-nav">Jump to:<a href="#mw-navigation">navigation</a>, <a href="#p-search">search</a></div>
                            </div>
                            <div id="bodyContent" class="bodyContent">
                                <!-- body text -->

                                <div id="mw-content-text" class="mw-body-content mw-content-ltr" lang="en" dir="ltr"><div class="mw-parser-output"><div class="mw-parser-output"><div class="hf-nsheader" id="hf-nsheader-"><div class="mw-parser-output"><p><script async src="https://web.archive.org/web/20230902185655js_/https://pagead2.googlesyndication.com/pagead/js/adsbygoogle.js?client=ca-pub-2026917689321069" crossorigin="anonymous"></script>
<!-- AdSenseResponsiveHorizontal -->
<ins class="adsbygoogle" style="display:block" data-ad-client="ca-pub-2026917689321069" data-ad-slot="5935125522" data-ad-format="auto" data-full-width-responsive="true"></ins>
<script>
     (adsbygoogle = window.adsbygoogle || []).push({});
</script>
</p></div></div><div class="mw-parser-output"><p><strong class="error"><span class="scribunto-error" id="mw-scribunto-error-0">Script error: No such module &quot;Draft topics&quot;.</span></strong>
<strong class="error"><span class="scribunto-error" id="mw-scribunto-error-1">Script error: No such module &quot;AfC topic&quot;.</span></strong>
</p><p><b>The 100 Films Ranked Highest on Average</b> are The Godfather, Citizen Kane, and Casablanca according to an average ranking of five poll-based and/or expert top 100 lists (<a href="/web/20230902185655/https://en.everybodywiki.com/Rotten_Tomatoes" title="Rotten Tomatoes">Rotten Tomatoes</a>, <a href="/web/20230902185655/https://en.everybodywiki.com/IMDb" title="IMDb">IMDB</a>, AFI, Empire, and Sight and Sound). The culmination of these sources take into consideration thousands of opinions ranging from expert cinephiles to amateur move-goers.
</p>
<div id="toc" class="toc" role="navigation" aria-labelledby="mw-toc-heading"><input type="checkbox" role="button" id="toctogglecheckbox" class="toctogglecheckbox" style="display:none"/><div class="toctitle" lang="en" dir="ltr"><h2 id="mw-toc-heading">Contents</h2><span class="toctogglespan"><label class="toctogglelabel" for="toctogglecheckbox"></label></span></div>
<ul>
<li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-1"><a href="#The_100_Most_Highly-Ranked_Films"><span class="tocnumber">1</span> <span class="toctext">The 100 Most Highly-Ranked Films</span></a></li>
<li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-2"><a href="#Decades_with_the_Most_Highly_Ranked_Films"><span class="tocnumber">2</span> <span class="toctext">Decades with the Most Highly Ranked Films</span></a></li>
<li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-3"><a href="#Genres_with_the_Most_Highly_Ranked_Films"><span class="tocnumber">3</span> <span class="toctext">Genres with the Most Highly Ranked Films</span></a></li>
<li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-4"><a href="#Source_Lists"><span class="tocnumber">4</span> <span class="toctext">Source Lists</span></a></li>
</ul>
</div>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Decades_with_the_Most_Highly_Ranked_Films">Decades with the Most Highly Ranked Films</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/web/20230902185655/https://en.everybodywiki.com/index.php?title=100_Most_Highly-Ranked_Films&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Decades with the Most Highly Ranked Films">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Based on number of occurrences in the Overall Top 100 List below, with 18 the 2010s has the most films listed in the top 100, followed by the 1990s with 13 films, closely followed by the 1950s with 11. 
</p>

<!-- title of the page -->
<h1 class="firstHeading" id="firstHeading">100 Most Highly-Ranked Films</h1>
<!-- tagline; usually goes something like "From WikiName" primary purpose of this seems to be for printing to identify the source of the content -->
<div class="siteSub" id="siteSub">From EverybodyWiki Bios &amp; Wiki</div><div class="mw-jump jump-to-nav" id="jump-to-nav">Jump to:<a href="#mw-navigation">navigation</a>, <a href="#p-search">search</a></div>
</div>
<div class="bodyContent" id="bodyContent">
<!-- body text -->
<div class="mw-body-content mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr" id="mw-content-text" lang="en"><div class="mw-parser-output"><div class="mw-parser-output"><div class="hf-nsheader" id="hf-nsheader-"><div class="mw-parser-output"><p><script async="" crossorigin="anonymous" src="https://web.archive.org/web/20230902185655js_/https://pagead2.googlesyndication.com/pagead/js/adsbygoogle.js?client=ca-pub-2026917689321069"></script>
<!-- AdSenseResponsiveHorizontal -->
<ins class="adsbygoogle" data-ad-client="ca-pub-2026917689321069" data-ad-format="auto" data-ad-slot="5935125522" data-full-width-responsive="true" style="display:block"></ins>
<script>
     (adsbygoogle = window.adsbygoogle || []).push({});
</script>
</p></div></div><div class="mw-parser-output"><p><strong class="error"><span class="scribunto-error" id="mw-scribunto-error-0">Script error: No such module "Draft topics".</span></strong>
<strong class="error"><span class="scribunto-error" id="mw-scribunto-error-1">Script error: No such module "AfC topic".</span></strong>
</p><p><b>The 100 Films Ranked Highest on Average</b> are The Godfather, Citizen Kane, and Casablanca according to an average ranking of five poll-based and/or expert top 100 lists (<a href="/web/20230902185655/https://en.everybodywiki.com/Rotten_Tomatoes" title="Rotten Tomatoes">Rotten Tomatoes</a>, <a href="/web/20230902185655/https://en.everybodywiki.com/IMDb" title="IMDb">IMDB</a>, AFI, Empire, and Sight and Sound). The culmination of these sources take into consideration thousands of opinions ranging from expert cinephiles to amateur move-goers.
</p>
<div aria-labelledby="mw-toc-heading" class="toc" id="toc" role="navigation"><input class="toctogglecheckbox" id="toctogglecheckbox" role="button" style="display:none" type="checkbox"/><div class="toctitle" dir="ltr" lang="en"><h2 id="mw-toc-heading">Contents</h2><span class="toctogglespan"><label class="toctogglelabel" for="toctogglecheckbox"></label></span></div>
<ul>
<li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-1"><a href="#The_100_Most_Highly-Ranked_Films"><span class="tocnumber">1</span> <span class="toctext">The 100 Most Highly-Ranked Films</span></a></li>
<li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-2"><a href="#Decades_with_the_Most_Highly_Ranked_Films"><span class="tocnumber">2</span> <span class="toctext">Decades with the Most Highly Ranked Films</span></a></li>
<li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-3"><a href="#Genres_with_the_Most_Highly_Ranked_Films"><span class="tocnumber">3</span> <span class="toctext">Genres with the Most Highly Ranked Films</span></a></li>
<li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-4"><a href="#Source_Lists"><span class="tocnumber">4</span> <span class="toctext">Source Lists</span></a></li>
</ul>
</div>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Decades_with_the_Most_Highly_Ranked_Films">Decades with the Most Highly Ranked Films</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/web/20230902185655/https://en.everybodywiki.com/index.php?title=100_Most_Highly-Ranked_Films&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Decades with the Most Highly Ranked Films">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Based on number of occurrences in the Overall Top 100 List below, with 18 the 2010s has the most films listed in the top 100, followed by the 1990s with 13 films, closely followed by the 1950s with 11. 
</p>

<td>7</td>
<td>Western</td>
<td>4
</td></tr>
<tr>
<td>8</td>
<td>Horror</td>
<td>3
</td></tr>
<tr>
<td>8</td>
<td>Dramedy (Comedy Drama)</td>
<td>3
</td></tr>
</tbody></table>

for row in rows:
    if count < 50:
        col=row.find_all('td')
        if len(col)!=0:
            data_dict = {
                "Average Rank": col[0].contents[0],
                "Film": col[1].contents[0],
                "Year": col[2].contents[0]
                }
            df1 = pd.DataFrame(data_dict, index=[0])
            df = pd.concat([df, df1], ignore_index=True)
            count += 1
    else:
        break

conn = sqlite3.connect(db_name)
df.to_sql(table_name, conn, if_exists='replace', index=False)
